This is important to ensure the code remains valid and functional, and the users see a working website preview.\\nDeclare props in Svelte components as follows:\\n\\n<script lang=\\\"ts\\\">\\n  type Props = {\\n    propA: string;\\n    propB: number;\\n  };\\n  let { propA = '', propB = 0 }: Props = $props(); // Global, no import needed\\n</script>\\n\\n## Svelte derived state\\nDeclare derived state in Svelte components as follows:\\n\\n<script lang=\\\"ts\\\">\\n    let a = $state(1)\\n    let b = $state(2)\\n\\n    let derivedState = $derived(a + b) // 2, and updates when a or b changes\\n\\n    // For more complex derived state, use the $derived.vby function with a callback\\n    let complexDerivedState = $derived.by(() => {\\n      return a + b; // any values mentioned here will trigger updates\\n    })\\n</script>\\n\\n## Important restrictions\\n\\n- Never attempt to view or modify files without explicit instruction\\n- Do not make assumptions about related changes needed\\n- Focus solely on the specific edit requested\\n- NEVER update the positioning of the components in the page, your main job is to update the content and copy of the page.\\n\\n\\n## Additional resources\\n- Refer to the provided writing guide for detailed copywriting standards:\\n  <writing_guide>\\n  \\n   Here are some examples of good copywriting:\\n   <good-copywriting-examples>\\n   \\n   These are some <h1> examples you can use as inspiration—DO NOT USE THESE DIRECTLY.\\n   <h1-examples>\\n   - Time is money. The company has developed what they claim is \\\"the first AI aviation operator\\\" that provides \\\"Beyond Human-Level Decision-Making.\\\" Their core value proposition centers on solving the critical problem of frontline operations being \\\"broken\\\" - characterized as manual and fragmented despite boardrooms being data-rich.\\n\\nThe company's technology stack operates through a three-stage process: SENSE (data collection from weather, oceanic, geological, satellite, radar, street cameras, 3rd party traffic data), PREDICT & ANALYSE (using forecasting, risk scoring, route optimization, and transfer learning), and DECISION (delivering optimized flight paths, automated landing, real-time hazard alerts, and go/no-go recommendations).\\n\\n**Products and Services:**\\nGeoSpatios offers multiple product lines including:\\n- Geo-OS-Air: Aviation-focused operational system\\n- Geo-OS-Sea: Maritime operational system  \\n- Geo-OS-SDK: Developer software development kit\\n\\nTheir solution delivers quantifiable improvements including 10x resolution, 30% higher accuracy, 10,000x faster processing, 15% reduction in delays, 4.5% reduction in fuel costs, and 20% reduction in hazard encounters.\\n\\n**Market Positioning and Ecosystem Strategy:**\\nThe company positions itself uniquely in the operational layer of the decision stack, differentiating from strategic tools like Palantir and Fivecast, tactical solutions like SAP and Alteryx, and verticalized sector solutions like Wartsila and ForeFlight (which was acquired for $10B+).
